  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f29bd061-eb96-4294-901a-31440d529fab'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText13351736110155820486" style="display:none">Half-human and half-Wyr, Pia Giovanni spent her life keeping a low profile among the Wyrkind and avoiding the continuing conflict between them and their Dark Fae enemies. But after being blackmailed into stealing a coin from the hoard of a dragon, Pia finds herself targeted by one of the most powerful—and passionate—of the Elder Races.<br /><br />As the most feared and respected of the Wyrkind, Dragos Cuelebre cannot believe someone had the audacity to steal from him, much less succeed. And when he catches the thief, Dragos spares her life, claiming her as his own to further explore the desire they've ignited in each other.<br /><br />Pia knows she must repay Dragos for her trespass, but refuses to become his slave—although she cannot deny wanting him, body and soul.</span>

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/30863-how-much-of-a-romance-is-it-i-love-the">How much of a romance is it? I love the Kate Daniels by Ilona Andrews and goodreads suggested Dragon Bound as a result...I love Vampire Academy and the alchemist books I like a bit of romance in my books but I also like a good urban fantasy story as well. Is Dragon Bound likely to be my cup of tea? I ask because it is so highly rated and there are 7 books in the series and also like a good solid read.</a>
</div>

The whole book revolves around the two main characters meeting and falling head over heels..or should I say tail. I have read ALL of the elder races books and they are excellent.             Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=2011-favorites">2011-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=pn-faeries">pn-faeries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=pn-dragons-wyverns">pn-dragons-wyverns</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=brain-candy">brain-candy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=pn-shapeshifters">pn-shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=read-2011">read-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=2011-publication">2011-publication</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=pnr-urban-fantasy">pnr-urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer179689675" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10866627512352799990"><b>4.5 stars</b> Oooo, smut smut smut smut smut. :D Is it terribly shallow to admit that I snapped up this book because I heard there was hot *whispers* <i>dragon sex</i> in it? I rarely read paranormal romances these days, but all of the reviews I saw for this book were raves, so I was wild with curiosity. Besides, I have a serious weakness for shapeshifters, which has sometimes led to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/173634905' rel='nofollow noopener'>disastrous reads</a> and sometimes led to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/165090316' rel='nofollow noopener'>really fun ones</a>. I'm happy to report that in this case, the book more than lives up to</span>
  <span id="freeText10866627512352799990" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b> Oooo, smut smut smut smut smut. :D Is it terribly shallow to admit that I snapped up this book because I heard there was hot *whispers* <i>dragon sex</i> in it? I rarely read paranormal romances these days, but all of the reviews I saw for this book were raves, so I was wild with curiosity. Besides, I have a serious weakness for shapeshifters, which has sometimes led to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/173634905" rel="nofollow noopener">disastrous reads</a> and sometimes led to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/165090316" rel="nofollow noopener">really fun ones</a>. I'm happy to report that in this case, the book more than lives up to the hype. <br /><br />The story is actually really good, and so well-plotted that in some ways, I'd say this is a lot closer to urban fantasy than your typical PNR; there's as much focus on the story as there is on the relationship. Pia, the central character, is very strong and principled. When we first meet her, she's just been coerced into stealing from a powerful dragon lord. Being a clever woman, she's stolen only a single penny, and she even left a note of apology in its place. Dragos doesn't care, however, and comes after her with all the force of his formidable powers and bristling with outrage and fury. Things begin to get interesting when they realize that Pia's coercion is actually part of a bigger political game between the Fae and the Elder Races...and when they discover their unwilling attraction to one another.<br /><br />And boy oh boy, is this relationship HOT. Dragos is a very, um, masculine guy and he's overwhelmingly attracted to Pia. The rumors of crazy dragon sex in this book were not exaggerated, but what I also love is that the relationship between them is portrayed with a great deal of respect and tenderness. They're strong as individuals, but they're so great together that you really want them to overcome all their obstacles and get their happily ever after. The secondary characters are also great, and the set-up for the next book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9665450.Storm_s_Heart__Elder_Races___2_" title="Storm's Heart (Elder Races, #2) by Thea Harrison" rel="nofollow noopener">Storm's Heart</a> is skillfully woven into the plot.<br /><br />Aside from a small bit of info-dumping in the beginning, this is an exceptionally well-written novel for the genre, and filled with humorous situations and hilarious one-liners. Several of my friends have pulled this out as a favorite quote, and I have to share it as well, because it just makes me giggle:<br /><br /><i>“So is that your long, scaly reptilian tail or are you just happy to see me?”</i><br /><br />Tee hee hee. How can you not laugh? This is a book that isn't afraid to poke fun at itself, which is a nice change from all the paranormal books that take their own mythology so seriously. Speaking of which, I also enjoyed the reveal of Pia's mysterious past and her...powers. It was a fun surprise and perfectly done.<br /><br />If you're inclined to read this sort of book, I can't recommend this enough--it's truly the best PNR book I've ever read. Every element that you could consider--the story, the magic, the characters, the romance, the sex, the writing--is absolutely terrific. You really couldn't ask for a more entertaining read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10866627512352799990" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText630730579332293517" style="display:none">Why did it take me so long to discover this series???? <br><br>Dragon Bound is the 1st book in Thea Harrison's Elder Races Series. The world that she's created is unique, fun and so cool. A world where shape-shifters, vampires, dragons and humans all trying to live together.<br><br>I loved this book. It had everything I want in a story. An unique and fresh plot, romance, tension, action, unforgettable characters, exotic settings and great dialogue.<br><br>Dragos &amp; Pia are my new favorite fiction couple. I adored them being together. Their chemistry is filled with hot sparks and sexual tension.....wow, off the charts!!! Their interaction was really fabulous.....the banter....I just loved their dialogue together..<blockquote>

<div id="review_146219244" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/146219244" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/146219244?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of paranormal/fantasy romance and stalkerific heroes</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=owned-copy">owned-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=faerie">faerie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-to-die-for">hero-to-die-for</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=fantasy-romance">fantasy-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=possessive-and-or-jealous-hero">possessive-and-or-jealous-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=alternate-dimension-or-world">alternate-dimension-or-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=plan-to-read-soon">plan-to-read-soon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=2020-action-heroines-yearly-challen">2020-action-heroines-yearly-challen</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=dragon">dragon</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer146219244" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7824835148727938172"><b>Reread on Audible done in May 2020:<br/><br/>I was inspired to do a reread since I finished <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10823507.Serpent_s_Kiss__Elder_Races___3_' title='Serpent's Kiss (Elder Races, #3) by Thea Harrison' rel='nofollow noopener'>Serpent's Kiss</a> and absolutely loved it. This book was as fantastic as I remembered it to be. It's strange to look back at a book nine years later. Some things struck me different, but I still really love this book. This time around, Dragos didn't seem as edgy as he did the first time. I guess it's because the edgy hero is fully in vogue now. I love Pia's sass and her tendency to talk to herself. The world-building </b></span>
  <span id="freeText7824835148727938172" style="display:none"><b>Reread on Audible done in May 2020:<br /><br />I was inspired to do a reread since I finished <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10823507.Serpent_s_Kiss__Elder_Races___3_" title="Serpent's Kiss (Elder Races, #3) by Thea Harrison" rel="nofollow noopener">Serpent's Kiss</a> and absolutely loved it. This book was as fantastic as I remembered it to be. It's strange to look back at a book nine years later. Some things struck me different, but I still really love this book. This time around, Dragos didn't seem as edgy as he did the first time. I guess it's because the edgy hero is fully in vogue now. I love Pia's sass and her tendency to talk to herself. The world-building is really excellent, and I can see why it was such a firm foundation for such a long series. I have rekindled my paranormal romance love and I'm off and running. <br /><br />Thoughts on the Audible version (free with Audible Escape): I enjoyed Sophie Eastlake's narration immensely. She is very good at voicing the various characters down to their specific timbre and cadence. I loved how she voiced Dragos (he definitely seems like an ancient, bossy, grumpy, sexy dragon). I would recommend checking it out.</b><br />**********************************************<br />Dragon Bound was an awesome book. I loved just about everything about it. I'm not even going to pretend that my favorite element wasn't Dragos, 'cause it was! I have an unnatural attraction to possessive, jealous, stalkerific heroes who are scary as heck, and Dragos is going on my list of favorite heroes of this type. I liked that although Pia started out as a thief who dared to steal from him, she became his own personal hoard. He acted like a dragon of old, used to having his way in all things. Even though he came on kind of strong, it was clear that he wouldn't do anything to hurt Pia. He cared enough to make sure that Pia was happy! He brushed her hair all the time! He was actually a softie underneath all that hard scaly dragon armor! Ms. Harrison knows how to write this kind of hero very well!<br /><br />Dragos is like a Harlequin Presents hero done well (with an intensity times one hundred). He is unbelievably wealthy, prominent and gorgeous. He is also immensely powerful. And he was done so well, there was never that incredulity factor where I have this sarcastic cheerleader moment in my head: "Yay, he is so awesome!" (rolls eyes). Dragos truly was awesome! Sick girl that I was, I liked that even though Pia found him hot and fell in love with him, she could still see he was a scary guy. Who doesn't like a guy who would give you the world, but he could also slaughter a whole army of enemies for you? Who's so jealous, he doesn't even like his crew touching you? (PSA awareness moment: Not okay in real life, but I like it in books. So shoot me!)<br /><br />I thought the world-building was really good. I loved the fact that this book has a strong fantasy element, equal to the romance. It wasn't just a backdrop for paranormal loving (which was verra nice, mind you). There was a lot of thought put into creating this world in which humans live alongside Wyr (shapeshifters) and Faerie folk of all kinds, and old magic is alive and well in this world, and into the adjacent magic realms. It seemed eminently plausible that one of the most powerful economic figures could be an ancient dragon. Don't I wish?<br /><br />Dragos is an awesome hero, and Pia is an equally awesome heroine. She is gutsy, intelligent, funny, and sweet. She never gave me the urge to ignore her and focus on the hero because I didn't like her. I loved her a lot. I could see myself having similar reactions to the strange circumstances she faces. I loved how utterly fearless (although inwardly quaking) she was when faced with the very scary Dragos, and especially at the end when she finds herself in a very rough situation. I loved her self-deprecating, humorous way of looking at the world, very down to earth and resourceful. I loved her secret heritage, and how Dragos cherished that part of her, and all parts of her. I felt tears brimming when she discovers what she truly is. (You have to understand that I was the little girl who was in love with Pegasus, Unicorns, and all mythical creatures. It was a sweet moment for this little girl who has never truly grown up inside).<br /><br />I loved Dragos' crew, especially Graydon (who reminded me of Butch from the Black Dagger Brotherhood series by JR Ward), and Tricks (a very hip elf who works as Dragos' PR rep and happens to be the true heir to Throne of the Dark Fae). How cool was it that his sentinels consisted of four gryphons and a tough female Harpy (she reminded me of my girl Xhex from the Black Dagger books). It was funny how Dragos came to life when Pia came around, and seeing how his crew reacted to the new Dragos. <br /><br />I don't think my review can really add anything because there are some great reviews out there of this book. I really did love everything about it. It was just hip enough (but not annoyingly so), the story and the fantasy elements were fantastic, there were many laugh out loud moments (this book was really funny), and some poignant moments. I loved the relationship between Pia and Dragos, and how they had to work at some things, but they weren't going to give up on being together. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ And my being a romance reader who likes babies, I was so happy that she even had that element. Not enough PNR books have pregnancy and babies in them for me (I know some readers hate that, but not me!) So I was glad she did have that in this book, and it was so cool how she did it. Definitely some 'aww' moments there.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I know I want to hug this book tight to my book-loving heart. I will put this out on my favorites shelf for a frequent reread. I can't wait to see what Ms. Harrison does in the next Elder Races books. She has a fan in me!<br /><br />My friends who said I would love this were right. High five!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7824835148727938172" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <td colspan="2">
    <div class="updateActionLinks">

      <span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_review_146219244'><a id="like_count_review_146219244" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/146219244?resource_type=Review"><span class="likesCount">141 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it gr-button gr-button--small" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F9637479-dragon-bound">Like</a></span>

<div id="review_157928536" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/157928536" />
    <a title="Shawna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna"><img alt="Shawna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574172018p2/1802746.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/157928536?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shawna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shawna" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna">Shawna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11141590-dragon-bound">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Any PNR fan!</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Shawna by: </span>
      RT Gold Medal &amp; author endorsements: Singh, Ward, Feehan, etc.
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=pnr-angeldemon-fae-magic-witch-misc">pnr-angeldemon-fae-magic-witch-misc</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=heroine-undeserving-of-awesome-hero">heroine-undeserving-of-awesome-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=rt-book-reviews-top-pick">rt-book-reviews-top-pick</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=a-all-time-favorite-hero">a-all-time-favorite-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=scifi-futuristic-fantasy-misc-pnr">scifi-futuristic-fantasy-misc-pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-cold-cruelbrute-dark-dangerous">hero-cold-cruelbrute-dark-dangerous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-antihero-gamma">hero-antihero-gamma</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-walking-hardon">hero-walking-hardon</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer157928536" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9984349859193850621">5+ stars – Paranormal Romance<br/><br/>A-M-A-Z-I-N-G! This time the author endorsements and reader hype are more than justified! I haven’t been this blown away by a paranormal romance debut or as energized and jazzed about a new PNR series in a long time. Not since diving into the addictive worlds of J.R. Ward’s bold, unbeatable <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i>, Lara Adrian’s mesmerizing <i>Midnight Breed</i>, Larissa Ione’s distinctive, dark <i>Demonica</i>, and Nalini Singh’s unique <i>Psy-Changeling</i> have I gotten such a thrill</span>
  <span id="freeText9984349859193850621" style="display:none">5+ stars – Paranormal Romance<br /><br />A-M-A-Z-I-N-G! This time the author endorsements and reader hype are more than justified! I haven’t been this blown away by a paranormal romance debut or as energized and jazzed about a new PNR series in a long time. Not since diving into the addictive worlds of J.R. Ward’s bold, unbeatable <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i>, Lara Adrian’s mesmerizing <i>Midnight Breed</i>, Larissa Ione’s distinctive, dark <i>Demonica</i>, and Nalini Singh’s unique <i>Psy-Changeling</i> have I gotten such a thrill from discovering a new paranormal romance series. <b>Dragon Bound</b>, the first book in Thea Harrison’s innovative, compelling <i>Elder Races</i>, gave me the same kind of high. I absolutely <i>loved</i> it!<br /> <br />Paranormal romance was my first foray into the vast world of romance after devouring the <i>Twilight Saga</i> and jonesing for more mature (and hotter!) fare and therefore will always have a special place in my heart. But after reading so many and finding blissful escape in other romance sub-genres that I love, I find I’m much more selective about PNR. I’m ecstatic that I’ve found a new series that’s got me excited about paranormal romance once again!<br /><br />Dragon shifter Dragos is one of the most ancient and powerful Wyr in the world and his rule over New York City is absolute. Nobody defies him, so he’s enraged and enchanted that a slip of a woman like Pia Giovanni would dare to steal from his prized treasure. Half-breed Pia was raised to closely guard her half-Wyr nature from other wyrkind, even if that means becoming a thief to protect her secrets from her ex-boyfriend’s threats of blackmail. The last thing she needs is to anger and arouse the fiercest Wyr predator in existence, but that’s exactly what happens when Pia invades a dragon’s private hoard. In exchange for a pardon and her very life, Dragos makes Pia a bargain she can’t refuse, and she finds herself thrust into the mysterious, dangerous world of magic she’s fought so desperately to avoid. If only she could resist the smoldering attraction that burns hotter than dragonfire between her and Dragos!<br /><br />Dragos...Be still my predator lovin' heart! YUM! He’s a hot, dangerous, possessive, dominating alpha hero used to getting anything and anyone he wants and always having everything his way, and he’s completely undone by his unfamiliar feelings for Pia. It was hilarious to witness his attempts to tame and gentle his beastly side for Pia, and sexy-as-all-get-out when he let the beast loose in their lovemaking. YOWZA! I loved Dragos and Pia together, and they had such funny, sexy banter and explosive chemistry. Pia’s resistance to Dragos annoyed me at times because I would have rolled over and begged for him, but her spunk was also charming.<br /> <br />One of the things that impressed me the most is how the author created such an imaginative, complex alternate modern society with so many fascinating varieties of magical beings (shifters, raptors, fae, elves, witches, goblins) and yet managed to avoid bogging down the story with too many heavy details and excessive world-building. There is an amazing cast of secondary characters that has me very eager for future books in the series. <br /><br />With a hotter-than-hell, possessive alpha hero, a quirky, feisty heroine, fast-paced action, clever dialogue, sexy banter, snarky humor, scorching sexual tension, strong, intriguing secondary characters, and steamy love scenes, <b>Dragon Bound</b> has everything I crave in a romance. It kept me thoroughly entertained! <br /><br />I highly recommend this for fans of Ward, Ione, Singh, Cole, Showalter, and Feehan, and anyone who enjoys an excellent paranormal romance. I can’t wait for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9665450.Storm_s_Heart__Elder_Races___2_" title="Storm's Heart (Elder Races, #2) by Thea Harrison" rel="nofollow noopener">Storm's Heart</a> to see what’s in store next for this thrilling series. <i>Big</i> 5 stars!<br /><br />A few of my favorite lines:<br /><br /><i>Oh my God, not only is he older than the Grand Canyon, but he’s like the pope and the Fae King and the president of the United States all rolled up into one. To some ancient cultures he had been a god. He was going to hurt her so bad before he killed her so dead, and all she could think of was how hot his kiss had been in the dream and how delicate the touch of his finger was as it traced down her body.<br /><br />For God’s sake. The male was injured and here she was ogling him like a pervert in a porn store.<br /><br />He rested his cheek against her head and rubbed her back. “I am cursed with a terminal case of curiosity,” he said. “I am jealous, selfish, acquisitive, territorial and possessive. I have a terrible temper, and I know I can be a cruel son of a bitch.” He cocked his head. “I used to eat people, you know.”</i><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9984349859193850621" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_205831078" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/205831078" />
    <a title="Flannery" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/652877-flannery"><img alt="Flannery" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312843258p2/652877.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/205831078?book_show_action=true">Sep 06, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flannery" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flannery" href="/user/show/652877-flannery">Flannery</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audio CD 9781452633640" href="/book/show/11715359-dragon-bound">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Dragon Lovers</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Flannery by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/2745288-wendy-darling">Wendy Darling</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/652877-flannery?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/652877-flannery?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/652877-flannery?shelf=i-wouldnt-read-on-the-t">i-wouldnt-read-on-the-t</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/652877-flannery?shelf=read-on-kindle">read-on-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/652877-flannery?shelf=audiobooks">audiobooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/652877-flannery?shelf=reviewed-2011">reviewed-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/652877-flannery?shelf=kcls">kcls</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/652877-flannery?shelf=read-in-2011">read-in-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/652877-flannery?shelf=half-listen-half-read">half-listen-half-read</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer205831078" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3781912774294581766">You know what is totally awkward? Listening to sexy books in audio format. There was a really great moment while I listened to this one when a friend of mine got in the car, I turned on the engine, and the narrator said something along the lines of “he caressed her breast as he pushed her legs further apart” and I frantically tried to switch to the radio, stumbling all over myself and hitting all the wrong buttons. Awkward City, population 1. Chalk that up as one more reason I prefer listening t</span>
  <span id="freeText3781912774294581766" style="display:none">You know what is totally awkward? Listening to sexy books in audio format. There was a really great moment while I listened to this one when a friend of mine got in the car, I turned on the engine, and the narrator said something along the lines of “he caressed her breast as he pushed her legs further apart” and I frantically tried to switch to the radio, stumbling all over myself and hitting all the wrong buttons. Awkward City, population 1. Chalk that up as one more reason I prefer listening to murder mysteries, YA, sci fi, and fantasy. Also, it feels weird being turned on while I’m driving around. BAM! How’s that for TMI on Goodreads? But you know what the ultimate libido killer is in books? The scrunchie. Oh, didn’t you know? Some contemporary authors are under the impression that despite the calendar reading 2011, we are somehow still living in the 1990s. Bare midriff shirts? Holy hell. Pretty soon I’m going to read a new release where the main character wears backwards overalls like Kriss Kross with one buckle undone, a hypercolor shirt, and Airwalks. <br /><br />I don’t want to harp on one tiny non-issue because this book was loads of fun. I initially started reading it with a friend but she blew past me because frankly, I’ve been a sucky reader with the attention span of a caffeinated toddler as of late. So I started it again as an audiobook and half listened, half read it the second time round. I’m a bit tired of fairies (scratch that, <i>totally</i> tired of them) but not at all tired of dragons yet so this worked really well for me. Plus, there are several more exciting Wyr kind in this book—Gryphons! Harpies! Thunderbirds! Goblins! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[A FRAKKING UNICORN!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>! Plus, you know, *cough* there may or <b>may</b> be some sexy dragon scenes. <br /><br />With a delightful sense of humor, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4443809.Thea_Harrison" title="Thea Harrison" rel="nofollow noopener">Thea Harrison</a> introduces us to Pia Giovanni, who has just stolen something from the hoard of the most powerful dragon in existence. Who hired her? How’d she do the seemingly impossible? What IS she? While the reader knows the answers to several of these questions (and can probably guess the answer to the last one if they’ve read enough in the genre), the well-paced plot and action scenes kept me entertained until the last page. Something that often bothers me in romance books is when a supposedly strong woman allows the man to treat her like property or doesn’t allow her to make decisions. There were several instances in this book when I was angered by some action or statement that Dragos made BUT Pia almost always stood up to him or addressed why it made her uncomfortable. She seemed realistically strong yet vulnerable and I didn’t find her needy or annoying, which is probably reason to celebrate. (or at the very least, continue reading the series…which I will do, probably next week!)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3781912774294581766" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2157609413" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15521134207276382820"><i>
  <b>“So, is that your long, scaly, reptilian tail, or are you just happy to see me?”</b>
</i><br/><br/>This is funny, paranormal smut. The guy is a dragon, and the girl shifts into something so OTT that you will have to laugh.<br/><br/><i><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508647587ra/24239468.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Is that my voice?</i><br/><br/>So, our girl, Pia, steals a penny from the dragon-man, Dragos, and he's pretty pissed off. Until he gets a whiff of her lovely girly smell. You all know by now that girls smell like sunshine and flowers and boys smell like leather and masculine trees. It's nature.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1508647587i/24239467.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>Could be wor</i></span>
  <span id="freeText15521134207276382820" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“So, is that your long, scaly, reptilian tail, or are you just happy to see me?”</b>
</i><br><br>This is funny, paranormal smut. The guy is a dragon, and the girl shifts into something so OTT that you will have to laugh.<br><br><i><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508647587ra/24239468.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Is that my voice?</i><br><br>So, our girl, Pia, steals a penny from the dragon-man, Dragos, and he's pretty pissed off. Until he gets a whiff of her lovely girly smell. You all know by now that girls smell like sunshine and flowers and boys smell like leather and masculine trees. It's nature.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1508647587i/24239467.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Could be worse. A lot worse.</i><br><br>Instead of killing her, he finds himself falling for her. But, he's not even a bit civilized, which is hilarious. <br><br><b>
  <i>She scratched an arm. “Did you kill the Fae horses?”<br><br> Dragos said in a cautious voice,“Was I not supposed to?” <br><br>She shrugged. “It just wasn’t their fault.” <br><br>“If it helps any, I was hungry and ate one.” <br><br>“I guess that does help some.”</i>
</b><br><br>Yeah, she's a vegan, and he's a carnivorous beast. It is a match made in heaven.<br><br>As long as you come into this book understanding that it's fluffy smut, you will have a good time with it. If you want a truly original storyline, a slow-burn romance, and amazing world-building, you need to keep shopping. As for me, I'm happy with this smutty little dragon-filled world for now. I'll keep with the series until I get bored.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1075675461" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7811543916347100329">✌ Buddy read with my <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148935-dust-off-your-machalo-it-s-time-for-another-buddy-read' rel='nofollow noopener'>MacHalo Freaks</a> ✌<br/><br/><i><b>Warning</b>: my reviewing mojo is still AWOL. This will therefore be a Super Crappy Review (SCR™). I really didn't feel like writing it, and tried to get out of it by subcontracting to one of my <s>ungrateful</s> dear friends, but not a single one of these <s>wimps</s> lovely people felt up to the task. So it's their fault if you have to suffer through this Piece of Crap (PoC™).</i><br/><br/><b><s>Confucianism</s> Confusion is me</b>. There usually are <b>two possible outcomes</b> when I read <b>Freaking PNR Novel</b></span>
  <span id="freeText7811543916347100329" style="display:none">✌ Buddy read with my <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148935-dust-off-your-machalo-it-s-time-for-another-buddy-read" rel="nofollow noopener">MacHalo Freaks</a> ✌<br><br><i><b>Warning</b>: my reviewing mojo is still AWOL. This will therefore be a Super Crappy Review (SCR™). I really didn't feel like writing it, and tried to get out of it by subcontracting to one of my <s>ungrateful</s> dear friends, but not a single one of these <s>wimps</s> lovely people felt up to the task. So it's their fault if you have to suffer through this Piece of Crap (PoC™).</i><br><br><b><s>Confucianism</s> Confusion is me</b>. There usually are <b>two possible outcomes</b> when I read <b>Freaking PNR Novels</b> (FPN™):<br><br>➽ 99,99% of the time, these <b>delightful pieces of literature</b> make me feel like this:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1461075600i/18820303.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>➽ 0,01% of the time, <s>a miracle happens</s> <b>I lose all judgement</b>, and end up feeling like this:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461339283ra/18855869.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Yeah, I get all pink and levitate and shake and stuff.</i><br><br><b>Well that was until today</b>. <i>Sorry, what was that? I finished reading this FPN™ almost a month ago, you say? Err, yes. And your point is? I shouldn't say "until today," because technically it's "until about a month ago," you say? Oh bloody hell, would you get off my back for once?! Would that be too much to ask?! Please don't bother to answer that, I think I know what you're going to say *sighs dramatically* Some friends you are.</i> Anyway, where was I? Oh yes, the two possible outcomes and all that crap. So the whole feeling either like this or like that thing lasted <b>
  <u>until the day I finished this book</u>
</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[← <i>happy now?!</i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. And until that glorious day, there had only been <b>two glorious types of glorious FPN™</b> for me: <br><br>① The Bloody Hell Feminism Committed Suicide Again I Need to Kill this Stupid Stupid Stupid Lame-A-Saurus Piece of Crap with Fire before it Claims more Victims You're Welcome (BHFCSAINtKtSSSLASPoCwFbiCmVYW™) type.<br><br>② The Oh What the Freaking Hell is Wrong with me I Think I Have Finally Lost it I just Gave 5 Freaking Stars to a Freaking PNR Novel Halp this is the End of the World as We Know it (OWtFHiWwmITIHFLiIjG5FStaFPNHtitEofWaWKi™) type.<br><br><b>All was fine and dandy</b> in my slightly bipolar PNR world when this book happened. I was anxiously awaiting to <b>rage and rant and dismember and stuff</b>. And what happened? This happened:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487581064i/22027755._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Introducing…the <b>So Bland and Dull it won't Even Cut through Butter Freaking PNR Novel</b> (SBaDiwECtBFPN™)! So <b>flat</b> and <b>lackluster</b> and <b>uninteresting</b> you won't suffer horribly while reading it! So <b>uninspired</b> and <b>unexciting</b> and <b>unstimulating</b> you will forget all about it two days after finishing it! So <b>unexceptional</b> and <b>unremarkable</b> and <b>un-pretty much everything</b> you will even forget to write a review for it! Be glad and rejoice, people, for this is <b>Pain Free PNR</b> (PFP™)! WOO HOO! YAY! ← <i>these expressions of joy and excitement might be slightly sarcastic.</i><br><br><b>Bloody hell, what a total rip-off this book was</b>. I mean, seriously?! PNR so insipid you don't even get a good rant out of it?! Who has ever heard of such a ridiculous thing?! <b>This is a disgrace</b>. This book brings shame to the glorious PNR genre. This will NOT do. Some things are just not done, Thea Harrison. The <b>Murderous crustaceans are not happy</b>, Thea Harrison. The Murderous crustaceans shall not condone such <b>scandalous behavior</b>, Thea Harrison. The Murderous crustaceans need to <b>vent and bitch</b> about something, Thea Harrison. They <u>will</u> get their <b>ragey fix</b> one way or another, Thea Harrison. <b>Be afraid, be very afraid</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1461392927i/18860928.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>PS</b>: this flat, lackluster, uninteresting, uninspired, unexciting, unstimulating, unexceptional, unremarkable, un-everything story is about dragons. It is kind of implied in the book title, but I thought I'd point it out anyway. <b>You're welcome</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<b>Pre-review nonsense</b>]<br><br>» <b>We have survived</b> fin-less, gill-less, scale-less, tail-less <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25018584-mermen" rel="nofollow noopener">mermen</a>.<br><br>» <b>We have survived</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12384423-the-haunted-vagina" rel="nofollow noopener">haunted vaginas</a>.<br><br>» <b>We have survived</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12806471-taming-my-teddy-bear" rel="nofollow noopener">plushophilia</a>.<br><br>» <b>We have survived</b> freaking <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22698881-the-corn-dildo-from-outer-space" rel="nofollow noopener">corn porn</a> (barely).<br><br>» <b>We even survived</b> a hilarious <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24748907-fire-down-below" rel="nofollow noopener">humor bestseller</a> (I still wonder how we made it through this one).<br><br>»» <b>Will we survive</b> if this proves to be yet another crappy dragon read? I doubt it. Not sure the damage caused by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2224451.Kiss_of_Fire__Dragonfire___1_" title="Kiss of Fire (Dragonfire, #1) by Deborah Cooke" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of Fire</a> can be undone.<br><br>I think we're going to need my <b>faithful Gustav's help</b> for this one.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456751581i/18272226.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>There, that should do it</b>.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="7811543916347100329" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1416945988" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1416945988" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1416945988?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=dragons">dragons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1416945988" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15785093132207673384"><b>
  <u>Dragos and Pia</u>
</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You took a 1962 penny,” Dragos said. His teeth were gritted. “You left a 1975 penny. It’s no replacement.”<br/>She stared at him. “Oh my God, it’s scary you noticed that.”<br/>“I know everything in my hoard and exactly where it is,” he told her. “Down to the smallest piece.”<br/>“You could go to a doctor, get checked out for OCD,” she panted. “There might be medication for that.”<br/>His chest moved in a silent laugh.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>My God! I love Dragos! And Pia. You cannot find easily a couple so w</span>
  <span id="freeText15785093132207673384" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>Dragos and Pia</u>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You took a 1962 penny,” Dragos said. His teeth were gritted. “You left a 1975 penny. It’s no replacement.”<br />She stared at him. “Oh my God, it’s scary you noticed that.”<br />“I know everything in my hoard and exactly where it is,” he told her. “Down to the smallest piece.”<br />“You could go to a doctor, get checked out for OCD,” she panted. “There might be medication for that.”<br />His chest moved in a silent laugh.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />My God! I love Dragos! And Pia. You cannot find easily a couple so well matched in PNR.<br />And how can you not love a book about a powerful dragon?<br />A book which starts with the stealing of a penny.<br /><br />Pia managed to infiltrate Dragos’ hoard and to steal a penny from him. She did that in order to save her douche ex-boyfriend by someone powerful (unknown in the beginning) who wanted something (anything) that belonged to Dragos Cuelebre, i.e. <br />*The most powerful being on Earth. <br />*A multi-billionaire tycoon. <br />*The boss of all the Wyrkind. <br />*Someone who used to be considered a god by many old civilizations.<br />*Born when the earth was formed and the sun shone with a different light<br />*The Great Beast.<br /><br />And now twenty-five years old Pia Giovanni has managed to draw the ancient Great Beast’s attention to her.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“No one takes what is mine.” His growl reverberated through the ground. He bared his teeth and bent down until he was nose to nose with her. “No one.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />What Pia needs to realize really soon is that Dragos has already included her in his collection:<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“She is mine.” Dragos bared his teeth, gold eyes flaring to lava. His growl shivered through the ground at her knees, and long fingers clenched on her wrist. He tensed and began to rise.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />The chemistry between Pia and Dragos is explosive:<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“There is not another entity in the world who would dare to act that way with me.”<br />She froze and the blood drained from her face.<br />His expression changed. He held a stiffened finger under her nose and said, “No! I did not mean that as a threat.”<br />Her lips trembled. “What did you mean then?”<br />He laid a hand on her cheek. It was so long it almost covered the length of her head. “You’re mine,” he said. “You can deny it, argue, throw fits, try to run away. But. You’re. Still. Mine.”<br />“That’s insane,” she whispered. “I have no idea what that means. I don’t belong to you or anyone else.”<br />“Yes, you do,” he told her. His thumb stroked her lips. “You are mine and I will keep you. I will not hurt you and I will protect you. And you’re beginning to trust me. All of that is a good thing.”<br />“I am not a piece of property, damn it!”<br />“But you are in my possession.”<br />She enunciated, “I think you are a lunatic.”<br />“Since you are too, that works well enough.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Pia has many secrets. Mainly she needs to trust Dragos enough and tell him what she really is. And then Dragos will help her.<br /> Dragos starts as a stubborn scary monster with OCD and as the book proceeds, he will melt for Pia.<br /><br />So this is an alternative world full of magic. A world where the Elder Races and humankind had lived together openly since the Elizabethan Age.<br />The Elder Races comprises of the Wyrkind, the Elves, both Light and Dark Fae, Vampires and Djinns. Every book more or less introduces an Elder Race.<br /><br />An amazing series. I cannot recommend it highly enough!<br />If you love PNR, or Urban Fantasy or Fantasy in general, you need to try this series!!! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15785093132207673384" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_147131010" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/147131010" />
    <a title="MelissaB" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1320046-melissab"><img alt="MelissaB" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1245899832p2/1320046.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/147131010?book_show_action=true">Feb 09, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MelissaB" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MelissaB" href="/user/show/1320046-melissab">MelissaB</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Paranormal Romance fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=2011-reads">2011-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=2020-reads">2020-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=favorite-paranormal-romance">favorite-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=shapeshifters">shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=elder-races-series">elder-races-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=2013-reads">2013-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=2015-reads">2015-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer147131010" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1513581265563402402">Wow! I loved this one! Dragon Bound was the best new paranormal that I have read in a long time, I am so glad to finally be excited about a new paranormal series.<br/><br/>Pia Giovanni is forced to do something that is basically suicidal - steal something from the most powerful dragon shifter in the world. She knows Dragos will react swiftly, most likely with a torturous death for her but she has no choice because of a spell and blackmail from a sleazy ex-boyfriend. Dragos is an ancient Wyr dragon shifter</span>
  <span id="freeText1513581265563402402" style="display:none">Wow! I loved this one! Dragon Bound was the best new paranormal that I have read in a long time, I am so glad to finally be excited about a new paranormal series.<br /><br />Pia Giovanni is forced to do something that is basically suicidal - steal something from the most powerful dragon shifter in the world. She knows Dragos will react swiftly, most likely with a torturous death for her but she has no choice because of a spell and blackmail from a sleazy ex-boyfriend. Dragos is an ancient Wyr dragon shifter who rules his kingdom with an iron fist. He is not happy that someone managed to steal from his treasure and hunts the thief with a savage intensity. However, he is intrigued with the wonderful scent on the note the female thief left behind.<br /><br />When Dragos catches up with Pia, their chemistry lights up the pages. He is fascinated by this half-breed human/Wyr who dares to stand up to him. They are both intensely attracted to each other, despite the fact Pia is afraid he is about to kill her. Dragos decides right away that she belongs to him. Despite Pia's protests that he can't just own a person, she is in for a losing battle against a powerful alpha like Dragos. So she does what she can - she stands up to him and fights his hold over her (while occasionally giving into the intense passion between them!). <br /><br />This book was such a fun, exciting romance. I loved Dragos, he was so alpha and possessive but he also tried to accommodate Pia and make her happy (in his life of course). Pia was a great heroine, she was strong and didn't just let Dragos run over her. She had a lot of secrets but she had good cause to keep her silence. Pia and Dragos were a great match and holy crap were they hot together! Yowza. I loved the story, it was exciting and well-written.<br /><br />If you are looking for a great paranormal romance, make sure to check this one out! It was a great story that I will be rereading in the future because I had a fun time reading about these characters. Highly recommended!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1513581265563402402" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_270678888" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/270678888" />
    <a title="Felicia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/666892-felicia"><img alt="Felicia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1437521850p2/666892.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/270678888?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Felicia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Felicia" href="/user/show/666892-felicia">Felicia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/666892-felicia?shelf=urban-paranormal">urban-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/666892-felicia?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/666892-felicia?shelf=vaginal-fantasy">vaginal-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer270678888" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8105027012293256199">Guys, this is 100% vaginal fantasy, and I enjoyed it. There were things I DID NOT enjoy about it, that take the stars down, but honestly I'm picking up the next book, so clearly I liked it and feel like this series can only get better. <br/><br/>I think my favorite thing was all the hugging. I seriously noticed I felt happy when the Dragon dude hugged the "so helpless I want to kick her" heroine. It's something that isn't in a lot of romance, that sort of casual affection between two people, and I really </span>
  <span id="freeText8105027012293256199" style="display:none">Guys, this is 100% vaginal fantasy, and I enjoyed it. There were things I DID NOT enjoy about it, that take the stars down, but honestly I'm picking up the next book, so clearly I liked it and feel like this series can only get better. <br /><br />I think my favorite thing was all the hugging. I seriously noticed I felt happy when the Dragon dude hugged the "so helpless I want to kick her" heroine. It's something that isn't in a lot of romance, that sort of casual affection between two people, and I really thought it was sweet and endearing. The world building in this is spotty, and the plotting uneven, I get it. The thousands of years old dragon talks completely inconsistently, sometimes very formally and sometimes like a dude you'd meet in a coffeeshop. There are corny bits. BUT the tone got way better the farther in the book it went. The main hero dude is a serious Cro-Magnon He-Man dude, but sometimes the heroine literally called it out spot-on, and it amused me to no end. I love how the author basically is telling the audience, yes this is seriously not PC to have a dude this controlling and chauvanist and jealous, but I'm writing this book about it anyway, because some base thing is going on here and I'm embracing it. I dunno, but despite its flaws I found the book refreshing.<br /><br />Lots of naughty scenes, very RRRRRRR rated btw. BE WARNED A DRAGON WILL COPULATE!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8105027012293256199" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_180299044" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/180299044?book_show_action=true">Jun 28, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa Kay" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa Kay" href="/user/show/2459470-lisa-kay">Lisa Kay</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer180299044" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8435668119563359845"><a href='http://s1205.photobucket.com/albums/bb438/LKC55/Decorated%20images/?action=view&current=Earthquake.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380352252i/705755.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><i>First read of paperback, July 22, 2011. See below for audiobook comment.</i><br/><br/>★★★★★ Yes, five full stars! One of the best paranormal/fantasy books I’ve read this year! I wanted to read it faster, but real life got in the way. As it was, I had it planned for a future “buddy read” and peeked at the first few pages. Three chapters later I was e-mailing my GR friend to hint around about moving this one up in our queue; luckily, she agreed. Ha! Indeed, she finished the book before I did. This is the fi</span>
  <span id="freeText8435668119563359845" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1205.photobucket.com/albums/bb438/LKC55/Decorated%20images/?action=view&amp;current=Earthquake.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380352252i/705755.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>First read of paperback, July 22, 2011. See below for audiobook comment.</i><br><br>★★★★★ Yes, five full stars! One of the best paranormal/fantasy books I’ve read this year! I wanted to read it faster, but real life got in the way. As it was, I had it planned for a future “buddy read” and peeked at the first few pages. Three chapters later I was e-mailing my GR friend to hint around about moving this one up in our queue; luckily, she agreed. Ha! Indeed, she finished the book before I did. This is the first one this year that we didn’t stick to our reading schedule, but zipped ahead, gobbling up the book like hungry carnivores, as fast as possible.<br><br>Anywayz, back to the book: For those of you who want more insights into their heroes, this is the one for you. Almost half the book is spent inside the hero’s, Dragos’, head. He is scary, arrogant, “stalkerific”<b>*</b>, possessive, and perplexed about his burgeoning feelings toward Pia. He is such a delightful, swoon-worthy “hero-in-pursuit”<b>**</b> to read about.<br><br>Pia is no slouch herself, even if she is a thief. She is dismayed at the ruination of her life – and she’s scared of Dragos. Despite her “nightmarish week” and one furiously pissed-off dragon on her tail, she is also funny, clever, generous, and a radiant mystery that is a wonder to uncover. She stole her way into my heart in no time flat.<br><br>If the bad guy is obvious from almost the beginning, who cares? The interaction and dialogue between Dragos and Pia alone is worth the price of the book. Escape plans? Joint efforts. Misunderstandings? They are talked out within a reasonable time. Love scenes? Toe-curling! Secondary characters? Amazing too. All in all, it kept me transfixed.<br><br>I highly recommend this book! It is imaginative, sweet, H.O.T., funny, and magical. Ms. Harrison has built a compelling, enchanted world parallel to ours that you’ll want to discover for yourself. Personally, I can’t wait for the next in the series. <br><br><b>*</b> “Stalkerific” is a term coined by the creative Lady Danielle; however, in true Pia inspired fashion, I stole it from her. :) <br><b>**</b> “Hero-in-Pursuit” is a term from the All About Romance special title listing they have for same; Lady Danielle has a bookshelf dedicated to them.<br><br><u>
  <b>Update:</b>
</u> May 5, 2012 (Comment on audiobook.) Loved this one so much in paperback, I had to get the audio and listen to it again. <b>Sophie Eastlake</b> does a nice job narrating this one; she sometimes has what I can only describe a sultry, lazy delivery. I picked up different things this time around. It is always interesting to hear how someone else will ‘act out’ a scene in their vocal delivery; not exactly how I had it in my head, but enjoyable enough. I would give the narration ★★★★☆.<br><br><i>Pia is supposed to look like the great <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greta_Garbo" rel="nofollow noopener">Greta Garbo</a>, “star and icon during Hollywood's silent and classic period.” (Wiki)</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379770746i/291404.jpg" width="200" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i><br>The Elder Races Series<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9637479.Dragon_Bound__Elder_Races___1_" title="Dragon Bound (Elder Races, <div id="review_1086804327" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1086804327" />
    <a title="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed"><img alt="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1455042547p2/22911953.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1086804327?book_show_action=true">Oct 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" href="/user/show/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed">Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=machalo-madness">machalo-madness</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=blame-the-br">blame-the-br</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=2016">2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=dragons">dragons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=2018">2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1086804327" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13865417796746318667">It happened, a dragon book we BR-ed that didn't suck dirty pond scum. Now my rating may be a bit high, but I will explain why (and I have low standards for dragon books anymore):<br/><br/>- The dragon guy was a badass monster. If you're a dragon, you should be badass and not a pansy dragon wimp like the ones in Dragon Tales on PBS. <br/>- Sexy times. Yes, there were sexy times in this book. That's important, because it's a paranormal novel and a) that's always present, b) seems like something that'd be part of</span>
  <span id="freeText13865417796746318667" style="display:none">It happened, a dragon book we BR-ed that didn't suck dirty pond scum. Now my rating may be a bit high, but I will explain why (and I have low standards for dragon books anymore):<br><br>- The dragon guy was a badass monster. If you're a dragon, you should be badass and not a pansy dragon wimp like the ones in Dragon Tales on PBS. <br>- Sexy times. Yes, there were sexy times in this book. That's important, because it's a paranormal novel and a) that's always present, b) seems like something that'd be part of a dragon's virile vitality, and c) dragons know how to seal the deal. I'm just going to assume all the dragons in the 1 star books previously read that were sexless, had erectile dysfunction. They should ask their doctor about some little blue pills. <br>- The heroine, Pia, had skillz. She had mad thieving skills, even if she was way too morally sound to use them. She also could take care of herself and didn't do TSTL things. I'm so tired of heroines having zero fighting/problem solving skills and running at every problem with all the finesse of a stampede of elephants, (I'm looking at you, Owl.) <br>- The heroine had a really neat wyr beast. <br>- The book contained a large variance of mythological and paranormal creatures. There were Elves (I totally pictured them all haughty like the elves in The Hobbit/LOTR), Light Fae, Dark Fae, gryphons, a harpy, vampires, goblins, a medusa, and a dragon. <br>- Death. Lots of good killing went on in this book. Yay. <br>- Dragos, the dragon, he used to eat people. Way to be an apex predator. ::claps::<br>- Dragos was super alpha male and all cowered before his ancient power. Kind of like Smaug crossed with Sauron, minus the whole end the world agenda. <br><br>The bad:<br>- Way too much info given. So many info dumps. <br>- Filler. This could've had tighter editing. <br>- One of the plot devices was very cliché. Blah. <br>- I don't like the name Pia. Sounds like peas, or similar to the word for feet in Romance languages. <br>- More dragons. <br>- Could've used more dead bodies. <br><br>For the most part, this book was good - the dragon was alpha scary and the heroine wasn't a crying pain in the ass. I particularly liked how Dragos was written. The author made him very lacking in human qualities and thought patterns. He had to learn them as he went along with the half human heroine. I enjoyed the times he'd blunder and get mad, while yelling at the heroine to tell him what he did wrong. <br><br>Now while I said this book was good, it's a reflection of how horrid the previous so called dragon books we've read have been that I rated this so highly. My standards for dragon novels is low. I was pretty happy after I read violence and sexy times, that's a huge improvement over previous books. Nothing has yet rivaled the stunning majesty that is the Dragon Kin series and I'm losing hope that anything ever will. <br><br><b>MacHalo BR, or maybe just with Sarah.</b> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456760193i/18273815._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="13865417796746318667" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1029831681" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1029831681" />
    <a title="Choko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27962805-choko"><img alt="Choko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475642755p2/27962805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1029831681?book_show_action=true">Aug 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Choko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Choko" href="/user/show/27962805-choko">Choko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=dragons">dragons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1029831681" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9149300540083408980"><b> *** 3.70 ***<br/><br/>A buddy read with my MacHalo Freaks!!!</b><br/><br/>This is very much a Paranormal Romance and the rating is very much exactly because of this fact. I had no idea what expect. I thought it would be either Urban or just a classic Fantasy. After all - DRAGONS!!! If anyone knows me, I am the biggest fan of Dragons there could possibly be.... I like them powerful, arrogant, growly, selfish, ruthless, vain, merciless, and fabulous in their dragonly majestic wonderfulness!!!! I like them all! <br/><br/>This book</span>
  <span id="freeText9149300540083408980" style="display:none"><b> *** 3.70 ***<br /><br />A buddy read with my MacHalo Freaks!!!</b><br /><br />This is very much a Paranormal Romance and the rating is very much exactly because of this fact. I had no idea what expect. I thought it would be either Urban or just a classic Fantasy. After all - DRAGONS!!! If anyone knows me, I am the biggest fan of Dragons there could possibly be.... I like them powerful, arrogant, growly, selfish, ruthless, vain, merciless, and fabulous in their dragonly majestic wonderfulness!!!! I like them all! <br /><br />This book has as the leading male one of those fabulous creatures, born as long ago as time itself. This has the trope which I mostly dislike in all PNRs - he is millions of years old, his love interest is in her 20s.... Yes, it could have been worse, she could have been a teenager and a virgin, which than the Stars, she is not!!! She is some mysterious type of shape shifting half-breed, who can bypass any locks and is terrified of her actual shape being discovered by anyone. So she is alone and constantly hiding in plain sight.... Until the big bad Dragon decides that she would be a perfect addition to his treasure hoard. Then her life explodes full of emotions - both positive and negative combined, and nothing is never the same.<br /><br />I enjoyed the world building, the different Fae creatures, and the Happily Ever After, which is the big sale for me in all Romance Genres. He could have been stronger, she could have been more consistent in her reactions, and the romance was predictable, but it gave me the smiles and relief that at least in books Happily Ever Afters are still possible!!! <br /><br />This is for all Romance lovers, but even more for those who like their love mixed with Magic and the Shifter classics. A fun read overall:-)<br /><br />Now I wish you all Happy Reading and may your life be enriched by every book you read!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9149300540083408980" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer551751665" class="readable"
